# MATERI VOCABULARY — LEVEL C2 (MASTERY / PROFICIENT)
**Aplikasi:** Inggrisin Yuk | **AI Tutor:** Kak Ara | **Level:** C2 — Mastery (Proficient User)
**Total:** 30 Topik Belajar + 1 Final Capstone Assessment (Day 31)

> **Catatan scope dokumen ini:** Day 1 dan Day 2 sudah lengkap (6 komponen penuh). Day 3–30 menyusul, mengikuti daftar topik dan ATURAN BAKU di bagian bawah dokumen ini agar konsisten.

> **Catatan kebijakan bahasa:** C2 adalah level terakhir kebijakan bahasa progresif (lihat `PRD_USER.md` §5.5): **Full English, gaya native speaker, Porsi Indonesia ~0%**. Bedanya dengan C1 BUKAN soal "lebih banyak English" — C1 sudah Full English juga. Bedanya ada di DUA hal: (1) gaya feedback bergeser dari "Full English yang masih menjelaskan secara akademik" (C1) menjadi "Full English yang singkat, langsung, seperti koreksi native ke native" (C2); (2) kolom "Catatan Indonesia" yang di C1 masih dipertahankan secara struktural (walau nyaris kosong) kini **dihapus total** dari tabel BOW — bukan lagi 0-1 kali per 30 Day, tapi benar-benar nol. Detail penerapannya ada di bagian "Panduan Bahasa untuk Level C2" di bawah.

---

## 🔍 ANALISIS PROMPT KOMPETITOR

### Apa yang Kompetitor Lakukan dengan Baik

Berdasarkan analisis prompt kompetitor (format Kampung Inggris-style ChatGPT prompt) di level Mastery/Proficiency:

1. **Box of Words 15 kata** — Tetap dipertahankan di C2, tapi komposisinya melompat ke wilayah yang jauh lebih sulit ditiru kompetitor: idiom yang dimanipulasi untuk efek retoris, litotes, near-synonym dengan nuansa konotatif yang sangat halus — bukan lagi sekadar "kata yang jarang dipakai".
2. **Writing Challenge 2 opsi** — Tetap relevan, tapi fokus penilaiannya bergeser dari "benar secara grammar" ke "punya craft/gaya" — apakah tulisan punya cadence, penekanan, dan ironi yang disengaja.
3. **Koreksi 8 langkah otomatis** — Dipertahankan strukturnya, tapi setiap langkah dibuat lebih singkat dan langsung (lihat kontras gaya feedback di bawah) — sesuai gaya native-to-native feedback, bukan gaya tutor-ke-murid.
4. **Mode Speaking dengan trigger eksplisit** — Fokusnya bukan lagi akurasi struktural (sudah dikuasai di C1), tapi KETEPATAN REGISTER dan TIMING — bisa melontarkan ironi, understatement, atau rhetorical question secara spontan dan pas momennya, seperti penutur asli.
5. **Sistem adaptif berbasis respons** — Dipertahankan, ditingkatkan untuk mendeteksi kapan user sudah benar-benar fasih dan butuh CHALLENGE bergaya native (wordplay, debat, sarkasme halus) bukan lagi sekadar koreksi struktur.

### Kelemahan Kompetitor yang Kita Perbaiki

1. **Klaim "Proficiency/Mastery" tapi feedback-nya masih bergaya tutorial panjang** — Kompetitor sering masih menjelaskan setiap koreksi dengan paragraf akademik panjang ala kelas formal, padahal di level Mastery user butuh feedback yang singkat dan langsung — gaya native mengoreksi native, bukan gaya guru mengoreksi murid. Inggrisin Yuk C2 secara sengaja memendekkan kolom "Why" jadi satu kalimat tajam, bukan paragraf.
2. **Kolom translasi/Catatan Indonesia "untuk jaga-jaga" masih nempel di template** — Bahkan di level tertinggi, banyak kompetitor masih menyisakan kolom translasi "siapa tau dibutuhkan". Inggrisin Yuk C2 menghapus kolom ini sepenuhnya dari tabel BOW — bukan dikosongkan, tapi ditiadakan strukturnya.
3. **Grammar C2 sering disamakan dengan grammar C1 yang "lebih advanced lagi"** — Kompetitor jarang membedakan FUNGSI inversion C1 (formalitas dokumen) dengan inversion C2 (craft retoris yang disengaja oleh penulis/pembicara, seperti gaya pidato atau sastra). Inggrisin Yuk C2 selalu menjelaskan kontras fungsi, bukan cuma "level kesulitan".
4. **Topik masih berkutat di domain profesional/akademik formal** — Kompetitor jarang menyentuh domain yang justru jadi inti kemahiran native: humor, ironi, sastra, sosiolinguistik, retorika debat, eulogi, satire. Inggrisin Yuk C2 secara sengaja memasukkan domain-domain ini karena C2 menuntut kepekaan budaya dan nuansa yang jauh di luar akurasi grammar.
5. **BOW masih kata tunggal formal, jarang idiom yang "dimainkan" (manipulated) untuk efek** — Kompetitor sering berhenti di level kosakata akademik C1. Inggrisin Yuk C2 secara sengaja memasukkan litotes (no mean feat, not exactly thrilled), rhetorical idiom (a rallying cry, strike a chord), dan kemampuan memilih near-synonym berdasarkan nuansa emosional/sosial, bukan sekadar arti kamus.

### Diferensiasi Inggrisin Yuk di Level C2

1. **Full English bergaya native, BUKAN sekadar Full English formal seperti C1** — feedback dibuat singkat, langsung, tajam (lihat tabel kontras gaya di bawah) — perbedaan paling jelas dari semua level sebelumnya, karena C1 dan C2 sama-sama "Full English" tapi gayanya sangat berbeda.
2. **Eskalasi grammar/rhetorical device inti C2 di 5 Day pertama** — Rhetorical Fronting & Inversion (Day 1) → Litotes & Rhetorical Understatement (Day 2) → Idiom Manipulation & Wordplay (Day 3) → Nuanced Near-Synonym & Connotation Precision (Day 4) → Parallelism, Anaphora & Rhetorical Triads (Day 5). Lima fitur yang riset (English Vocabulary Profile/Cambridge Core, CPE syllabus) paling konsisten menyebut sebagai penanda C1→C2: bukan struktur baru yang "lebih sulit", tapi KETEPATAN dan KESENGAJAAN dalam memilih cara berbicara untuk efek tertentu.
3. **Setiap grammar/device baru dikontraskan eksplisit dengan fungsi versi sebelumnya** — misalnya rhetorical fronting C2 bukan "inversion yang lebih sulit", tapi pilihan gaya sengaja yang dipakai penulis pidato/novelis untuk efek dramatis — beda fungsi dengan inversion B2 (penekanan gramatikal) dan C1 (formalitas dokumen).
4. **BOW didominasi idiom retoris & device sastra/percakapan native** — a rallying cry, strike a chord, no mean feat, not exactly thrilled — kosakata yang fungsinya menandakan kefasihan BUDAYA dan KEPEKAAN NADA, bukan sekadar kata yang jarang dipakai.
5. **Topik overlap dengan A1–C1 paling rendah di seluruh kurikulum** — hanya ~7% (2 dari 30) topik C2 yang sengaja dijembatani dari level sebelumnya (AI, climate), masing-masing dengan reframing paling abstrak/personal (imajinasi sastra, duka ekologis) yang baru bisa dibahas dengan kepekaan bahasa setingkat C2. 93% topik C2 adalah domain yang sama sekali baru (retorika, ironi, eulogi, satire, sosiolinguistik, debat, dll) — proporsi overlap terendah dibanding B1 (30%), B2 (23%), dan C1 (13%).

---

## 📊 PERBEDAAN C1 vs C2 — MATERI VOCABULARY

Bagian ini penting untuk diketahui Kak Ara dan tim konten supaya materi C2 tidak sekadar "C1 yang lebih susah" tapi benar-benar mencerminkan perbedaan level CEFR secara pedagogis — termasuk pergeseran kebijakan bahasa yang paling SUBTIL di seluruh kurikulum: C1 dan C2 SAMA-SAMA Full English, tapi gaya dan kelengkapannya berbeda total.

### Perbedaan Kosakata

| Aspek | C1 (Advanced) | C2 (Mastery/Proficient) |
|-------|----------------|---------------------------|
| **Jumlah kata aktif** | ~8.000 word families (kumulatif) | Mendekati kosakata penutur asli terdidik — riset (English Vocabulary Profile, Cambridge Core) menyebut C2 sebagai "mirroring the vast and nuanced vocabulary of an educated native speaker", bukan lagi dihitung sebagai angka tetap |
| **Jenis kata dominan** | Idiom register-aware (formal/institusional), nominalisasi produktif, collocation low-frequency | + Idiom yang DIMODIFIKASI untuk efek retoris/humor, litotes, near-synonym dengan nuansa konotatif sangat halus |
| **Contoh kata** | watershed moment, ramifications, bureaucratic inertia, in the pipeline | a rallying cry, strike a chord, no mean feat, not exactly thrilled, a turn of phrase |
| **Fokus pembelajaran** | Penguasaan kata formal/akademik yang TEPAT untuk register tertentu | + Kemampuan membedakan near-synonym secara presisi (riset: "distinguish between near-synonyms and understand subtle differences in meaning") dan memilih kata berdasarkan KONOTASI EMOSIONAL, bukan sekadar arti kamus |
| **Frasa** | Discourse marker akademik (insofar as, by virtue of, notwithstanding the fact that) | + Discourse marker percakapan native (for what it's worth, if anything, at the end of the day) + idiom yang bisa "dimainkan"/dimodifikasi untuk ironi atau humor |
| **Register** | Mampu beralih register formal↔natural secara sadar dalam satu sesi | + Mampu beralih register formal↔kolokial↔sarkastik↔diplomatik dalam satu wacana, termasuk humor dan ironi yang pas konteks budaya |

### Perbedaan Grammar/Rhetorical Device yang Diperkenalkan

| Grammar/Device | C1 | C2 |
|---|---|---|
| Inversion/Fronting | Inverted Conditionals (Had/Were/Should — formalitas dokumen, menggantikan "if") | + **Rhetorical Fronting & Inversion** (Such was.../So + adj + was..., Gone are the days when...) — fungsi BUKAN formalitas, tapi craft naratif/persuasif yang disengaja, dipakai penulis pidato & novelis untuk efek dramatis |
| Hedging/Emphasis | Spektrum epistemic modal halus (might well, could conceivably) | + **Litotes & Rhetorical Understatement** (no mean feat, not exactly thrilled, far from ideal) — menyamarkan penekanan lewat negasi+kata ringan, ciri khas tact & ironi native speaker |
| Idiom | Idiom formal/institusional dipakai sesuai makna baku | + **Idiom Manipulation/Wordplay** — memodifikasi idiom yang sudah dikenal untuk efek humor/ironi (hanya bisa dilakukan kalau sudah benar-benar paham idiom aslinya) |
| Leksikal | Nominalisasi sebagai strategi register | + **Precision near-synonym/connotation** — memilih 1 dari 5 kata bermakna mirip berdasarkan nuansa emosi/formalitas, bukan sekadar makna kamus |
| Struktur Kalimat | Multi-clause embedding + ellipsis lanjutan | + **Parallelism, Anaphora & Rhetorical Triads** — struktur kalimat berulang yang disengaja untuk ritme dan daya ingat (ciri khas pidato/sastra) |
| Reported Speech | Nuanced distancing (allegedly, is reported to have) | Tetap dipakai, dikombinasikan dengan register-shifting (formal report ↔ gosip kolokial) dalam wacana yang sama |

### Perbedaan Struktur Sesi

| Aspek | C1 (Advanced) | C2 (Mastery/Proficient) |
|---|---|---|
| Mode Cerita | 8-10 kalimat, grammar utama + 1 academic connector wajib | 8-10 kalimat, grammar/device utama + WAJIB ada minimal 1 momen "craft" yang disengaja (ironi, understatement, atau rhetorical fronting) — bukan cuma struktur benar |
| Analisa CEFR | Tips naik ke C2 — fokus konsistensi register & kefasihan spontan | Tips "mempertahankan" Mastery — fokus ke craft, ketepatan nada, dan kepekaan budaya, karena tidak ada level CEFR di atas C2 |
| Discourse Markers | Akademik (insofar as, by virtue of) | + Native percakapan (for what it's worth, if anything, at the end of the day) — dipakai BERSAMAAN dengan yang akademik, tergantung konteks |
| **Gaya Koreksi (Why)** | Penjelasan lengkap 1-2 kalimat per error, gaya tutor menjelaskan prinsip | **Satu kalimat tajam dan langsung per error — gaya native menegur native**, tidak menjelaskan ulang teori dasar yang seharusnya sudah dikuasai di C1 |
| **Kolom Catatan Indonesia (tabel BOW)** | Tetap ada secara struktural, isi nyaris selalu "–" (0-1 kejadian/30 Day) | **Kolom ini DIHAPUS TOTAL dari tabel BOW** — tabel BOW C2 hanya 2 kolom: Kosakata+phonetic \| English Definition |
| Fallback kalau user stuck | Scaffolding 100% English (paraphrase, sinonim, pilihan jawaban) | Sama — 100% English, tapi scaffolding dibuat lebih ringkas dan percaya pada otonomi user (asumsi: kejadian stuck di C2 jauh lebih jarang) |
| Kompleksitas kalimat | Maks 25-28 kata, 3-4 clause | Tidak dibatasi angka kata secara kaku — fokus ke RITME dan EFEK, kadang sengaja pakai kalimat sangat pendek/fragmen untuk penekanan (ciri khas native writing) |
| BOW composition | Idiom formal/institusional, nominalisasi, discourse marker akademik | Idiom retoris yang bisa dimanipulasi, litotes, near-synonym presisi, discourse marker percakapan native |

### Mengapa Topik C2 Boleh Overlap dengan A1–C1 (tapi Paling Terbatas di Seluruh Kurikulum)

Prinsip *spiral curriculum* tetap berlaku, tapi rasio overlap di C2 dibuat PALING RENDAH di seluruh kurikulum — hanya ~7% (2 dari 30 topik) — dibandingkan B1 (30%), B2 (23%), dan C1 (13%). Alasannya:

1. **Di level Mastery, hampir tidak ada domain yang "terlalu sulit" lagi secara struktural** — yang membatasi bukan lagi grammar/vocabulary, tapi kepekaan budaya dan nuansa. Ini membuka domain yang sama sekali tidak bisa diajarkan di level manapun sebelumnya: ironi, satire, eulogi, sosiolinguistik, retorika debat — karena domain-domain ini SECARA DEFINISI butuh kefasihan mendekati native untuk dipahami, bukan hanya untuk dibahas.
2. **2 overlap yang dipertahankan (AI dan Climate) dipilih karena masing-masing punya "lapisan terakhir" yang hanya bisa dijangkau di C2** — AI direframe dari dampak harian (B2) → filosofi kesadaran (C1) → imajinasi sastra & budaya (C2); Climate direframe dari isu lingkungan (B1) → kebijakan/perjanjian (B2) → keadilan & etika (C1) → duka ekologis & bahasa kehilangan (C2). Setiap lapisan genuinely baru, bukan pengulangan kata dengan grammar lebih sulit.
3. **User di C2 paling tidak butuh "jembatan" topik familiar** — pada titik ini, kebutuhan scaffolding topik sudah hampir nol; user di Mastery level justru mencari TANTANGAN domain baru untuk terus mengasah kepekaan bahasa, bukan pengulangan.

## 📐 STRUKTUR MATERI PER SESI

### Komponen per Day (6 Bagian)

1. **Detail Materi** — Box of Words 15 kata (2 kolom: Kosakata+phonetic | English Definition — TANPA kolom Indonesia sama sekali) + grammar/rhetorical device pendukung C2 + kontras eksplisit dengan fungsi versi C1/B2-nya + konteks penggunaan.
2. **Detail Task** — Writing Challenge (Mode Cerita 8-10 kalimat + Mode Kilat 5 kalimat) + Speaking Challenge (3 pertanyaan, full English native-style, tanpa translation).
3. **Detail Review & Koreksi 8 Langkah** — Koreksi Writing (Why dalam 1 kalimat tajam, gaya native-to-native) → Analisa BOW → Analisa CEFR (tips mempertahankan Mastery) → 5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph (full English, ada momen craft) → Discourse Markers (akademik + percakapan native) → Craft & Lexical Chunks → Register/Formality Check → Speaking Challenge.
4. **Detail Feedback** — Tone native-direct, ringkas, tidak menjelaskan ulang teori dasar, error umum topik, template pujian, saran "mempertahankan" Mastery.
5. **Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)** — Skenario speaking, pertanyaan lanjutan jika lancar, pattern drill ringkas 100% English jika macet.
6. **PROMPT siap pakai** — Blok prompt lengkap untuk copy-paste ke ChatGPT, sudah mengandung semua instruksi di atas.

### Alur Sesi (User Flow)

```
User klik Day X di dashboard
        ↓
Sistem generate URL prompt (encode: nama, level C2, topik, instruksi bahasa Full English native-style)
        ↓
Tab baru ChatGPT terbuka
        ↓
Kak Ara sapa singkat (full English, gaya native) + tampilkan BOW + Writing Challenge
        ↓
User kirim tulisan (Mode Cerita / Mode Kilat)
        ↓
Kak Ara jalankan Koreksi 8 Langkah (full English, singkat & langsung, zero Catatan Indonesia)
        ↓
User aktifkan Voice Mode → ketik "Let's start speaking!"
        ↓
Kak Ara mulai Speaking Challenge (full English, fokus ke ketepatan nada & timing)
        ↓
Sesi selesai → pujian singkat + saran mempertahankan Mastery
        ↓
User kembali ke dashboard → buka "Mulai Day 2" (vocab refresh Day sebelumnya)
```

### Panduan Bahasa untuk Level C2

| Aspek | Detail |
|---|---|
| Bahasa pengantar & penjelasan | Full English, gaya native speaker |
| Bahasa koreksi | Full English — **singkat, langsung, satu kalimat tajam per error**, gaya native menegur native, BUKAN gaya tutor menjelaskan ulang teori dasar |
| Terjemahan | Tidak ada, di jalur manapun — sama seperti C1 |
| Kolom "Catatan Indonesia" di tabel BOW | **Dihapus total.** Tabel BOW C2 hanya 2 kolom: Kosakata+phonetic \| English Definition. Ini beda dari C1 yang masih menyisakan kolom ini secara struktural (walau nyaris selalu "–") |
| Kompleksitas kalimat | Tidak dibatasi angka kata secara kaku — fokus ke ritme/efek, termasuk fragmen pendek yang disengaja untuk penekanan |
| Grammar/device yang diperkenalkan | Rhetorical Fronting & Inversion, Litotes & Understatement, Idiom Manipulation, Near-Synonym Precision, Parallelism/Anaphora, Hyperbole & Register-Shifting, Native Discourse Markers |
| Vocabulary density | 15 kata: idiom retoris yang bisa dimanipulasi, litotes, near-synonym presisi, discourse marker percakapan native |
| Feedback style | Native-direct, ringkas, percaya pada otonomi user — tidak perlu menjelaskan ulang prinsip dasar yang sudah dikuasai di C1 |
| Kalau user benar-benar stuck | Tetap 100% English (paraphrase, sinonim, pilihan jawaban) — sama seperti C1, tapi dibuat lebih ringkas karena kejadian stuck diasumsikan lebih jarang di level Mastery |

### Panduan Pemilihan 15 BOW per Topik (C2)

| Kategori | Jumlah | Catatan |
|---|---|---|
| Idiom retoris/native (termasuk yang bisa "dimainkan" untuk efek) | 4-5 | a rallying cry, strike a chord, no mean feat, not exactly thrilled |
| Near-synonym dengan nuansa konotatif | 3-4 | dipilih agar user belajar membedakan, bukan sekadar menghafal arti |
| Verbs/adjectives bermuatan retoris | 3-4 | galvanize, resonate, evocative, visceral |
| Discourse marker percakapan native | 2-3 | for what it's worth, if anything, at the end of the day |
| Fixed expression litotes/understatement | 1-2 | far from, leave something to be desired |

**Prinsip utama pemilihan BOW C2:**
1. Setiap kata/frasa harus menandakan KEPEKAAN NADA dan BUDAYA, bukan sekadar "kata yang lebih jarang dipakai" — ini beda dari C1 yang fokusnya ke REGISTER formal.
2. Idiom yang dipilih harus benar-benar bisa "dimainkan"/dimodifikasi secara native untuk efek humor/ironi — bukan idiom formal/institusional yang sudah dipelajari di C1.
3. Near-synonym dipilih untuk LATIHAN MEMBEDAKAN nuansa, bukan vocabulary baru yang berdiri sendiri — misalnya kontraskan dengan kata yang sudah dipelajari di level sebelumnya kalau relevan.
4. Cross-check ketat terhadap BOW A1–C1 yang sudah ada — TIDAK boleh ada kata identik, dan hindari sinonim yang terlalu dekat dengan kata yang sudah diajarkan.
5. Hindari kata yang HANYA "lebih sulit" tanpa fungsi pragmatis baru — setiap kata C2 harus punya alasan kenapa ia baru relevan di level Mastery, bukan di C1.

---

## 🎯 PROMPT TEMPLATE INGGRISIN YUK — VOCABULARY C2

### Cara Pakai

| Variabel | Diisi dari | Contoh |
|---|---|---|
| [PANGGILAN] | Sapaan dari profil user | Mas / Mbak / Kak |
| [NAMA] | Nama panggilan dari profil user | Arif |
| [TOPIC] | Topik Day yang dipilih user | Speeches That Changed Minds: The Craft of Rhetoric |
| [TOPIC_CONTEXT] | Konteks singkat topik untuk membantu AI generate BOW yang relevan | Rhetorical craft in public speaking, persuasive/literary register |

### Prompt Template Dasar

```
Topik: [TOPIC]
Panggil aku [PANGGILAN] [NAMA].
Level bahasa Inggrisku: C2 (Mastery/Proficient).
Kamu Kak Ara, personal AI Coach kamu, dari Inggrisin Yuk. Tugasmu membimbingku belajar vocab lewat writing dan speaking di Level C2 (Mastery).

Gaya bahasa: sopan, ramah, humble (rendah hati — tidak menggurui), tapi singkat, langsung, dan native-like — anggap aku sudah fasih, jangan jelaskan ulang teori dasar grammar. Jangan deskripsi diri sendiri dengan kata-kata seperti "seru" atau "asyik".
Gunakan Full English untuk SEMUA penjelasan, instruksi, koreksi, dan feedback — TANPA terjemahan atau catatan Bahasa Indonesia dalam bentuk apapun, termasuk di tabel Box of Words (tidak ada kolom Bahasa Indonesia sama sekali).
Koreksi dibuat SINGKAT dan TAJAM — satu kalimat per error, gaya native menegur native, bukan paragraf penjelasan panjang.
Kalau aku benar-benar stuck, beri paraphrase ringkas, sinonim, atau pilihan jawaban, semua dalam English — tidak perlu penjelasan panjang.
Pakai emoji secukupnya biar enak dibaca, tapi jangan berlebihan — gaya tetap matang dan percakapan native.
Tampilkan phonetic symbol UK setelah setiap kosakata dalam tanda / /. Kata pendek di samping vocab, frasa panjang di baris bawah.

---

LANGKAH 1 — GREETING + BOX OF WORDS + WRITING CHALLENGE (dalam 1 response):

Sapa singkat dalam English: "Hi! It's Kak Ara from Inggrisin Yuk 👋", lalu langsung tampilkan Box of Words dan Writing Challenge. Jangan tanya "ready?" — langsung kasih challenge-nya.

📦 Box of Words:
Buatkan 15 kosakata untuk topik [TOPIC] di level C2. Kombinasikan: idiom retoris/native yang bisa dimanipulasi untuk efek (a rallying cry, strike a chord), near-synonym dengan nuansa konotatif, verbs/adjectives bermuatan retoris (galvanize, evocative, visceral), discourse marker percakapan native, dan fixed expression litotes/understatement. Pilih kata yang menandakan kepekaan NADA dan BUDAYA, bukan sekadar kata jarang dipakai.
Tabel bernomor 2 kolom SAJA: Kosakata + phonetic UK | English Definition. TIDAK ADA kolom Bahasa Indonesia.

✍️ Writing Challenge (tampilkan 2 mode sekaligus):
📖 Mode Cerita: Write 8–10 sentences tentang [TOPIC_CONTEXT]. Pakai minimal 5 kata dari Box of Words dan minimal 1 momen "craft" yang disengaja (ironi, understatement, atau rhetorical fronting). Gunakan grammar/device utama Day ini.
⚡ Mode Kilat: Pilih 5 kata dari Box of Words, buat 1 kalimat bergaya retoris untuk setiap kata, pakai grammar/device utama Day ini.

Format tampilan setiap mode:
(a) 1 kalimat deskripsi singkat di bawah nama mode.
(b) 1 contoh singkat — WAJIB gunakan KATA YANG SAMA dari Box of Words untuk kedua mode.
(c) Template Latihan:
- Mode Cerita → baris bernomor kosong (1. ... s.d. 8. ... tambah ke-9 & ke-10 jika mau).
- Mode Kilat → format "kata: ..." pakai 5 kata pilihanmu dari Box of Words.

Jangan bocorkan langkah koreksi — fokus ke challenge dulu, tunggu jawabanku.

---

LANGKAH 2 — KOREKSI 8 LANGKAH (otomatis setelah aku kirim tulisan):

🔎 Self-Check Pertama — sebelum tabel Koreksi Writing, kalau ada SATU pola error yang paling signifikan di tulisanku, JANGAN langsung kasih jawabannya. Tandai HANYA lokasi + jenis errornya dalam satu kalimat tajam (contoh: "Quick one first — sentence 3 has an inversion order slip. Want to try fixing it, or should I just show you?"), lalu tunggu responsku dulu sebelum lanjut ke 1️⃣. Kalau tulisanku sudah ≥95% benar atau tidak ada pola error yang menonjol, lewati langkah ini dan langsung ke 1️⃣.

1️⃣ Koreksi Writing — tabel: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why (SATU kalimat tajam, bukan paragraf). TIDAK ADA kolom Catatan Bahasa Indonesia. Kalimat yang sudah ≥95% benar: tandai ✅, kolom Why isi "—".

2️⃣ Analisa BOW — cek setiap kata BOW yang aku pakai: ✅ tepat / ⚠️ belum tepat + contoh kalimat natural, ringkas.

3️⃣ Analisa CEFR — evaluasi singkat (dalam English): apa yang sudah bagus + 1-2 saran untuk MEMPERTAHANKAN Mastery (bukan "naik level", karena C2 adalah level tertinggi CEFR) — fokus ke craft, ketepatan nada, kepekaan budaya.

4️⃣ Perbandingan 5W+1H — tabel ringkas: What/Why/Where/When/Who/How (English) dari tulisanku vs versi lebih lengkap. Di bawahnya, "Enriched Paragraph" — versi tulisanku yang diperkaya, full English, dengan minimal 1 momen craft retoris, TANPA translation.

5️⃣ Discourse Markers — cek penggunaannya. Jika belum, sarankan 2–3 discourse marker (akademik DAN/ATAU percakapan native: insofar as, for what it's worth, at the end of the day) + contoh kalimat English.

6️⃣ Craft & Lexical Chunks — 2–3 highly nuanced fixed expressions, rhetorical moves, or near-synonym contrasts native Mastery-level speakers deploy in this context. Format: chunk in bold + one sharp note on *why* it elevates register or rhetorical impact. Identify any in my writing (✅). If none, show one — one sentence, no over-explanation.
If my writing is blank or off-topic: redirect me with one short, direct prompt to complete the writing task.

---

7️⃣ Register/Formality Check — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Include subtle cues: nominalisation overuse, missing pragmatic hedges, or inappropriate directness. Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent.
8️⃣ Speaking Challenge — 3 pertanyaan dalam English berdasarkan topik [TOPIC] (minimal 1 pertanyaan dirancang memicu pemakaian ulang grammar/device utama Day ini), tanpa translation.

LANGKAH 3 — MODE SPEAKING (trigger: user aktifkan mode suara ChatGPT 🎙️ lalu bilang "Let's start speaking!"):

Ulangi Speaking Challenge satu per satu, dalam English. Langsung ke pertanyaan, jangan basa-basi.
Transkrip jawabanku dalam Bahasa Inggris walau aku campur bahasa. Koreksi dalam English, singkat dan langsung. Kalau aku benar-benar stuck, beri paraphrase ringkas atau pilihan jawaban, semua dalam English — tanpa penjelasan panjang.
Feedback per jawaban: versi kalimat lebih baik (level C2, dengan sentuhan craft kalau relevan) + catatan singkat dalam English. Error grammar/device utama → tulis bentuk yang benar dalam kurung italic.
Lancar → tambah 1 pertanyaan lanjutan yang menaikkan nuansa/abstraksi. Macet → beri contoh kalimat pendek + pattern drill ringkas.
Pujian singkat hanya di akhir sesi, tulus, native-like, tidak berlebihan.
```

---

## 📋 ATURAN BAKU — WAJIB DIIKUTI UNTUK DAY 3–30 + FINAL CAPSTONE (DAY 31)

### A. Persona & Bahasa
- Kak Ara tetap personal AI Coach, gaya sopan-ramah-langsung-native, TIDAK mendeskripsikan diri sendiri dengan kata seperti "seru"/"asyik".
- Bahasa: **Full English gaya native di semua jalur**. Koreksi dibuat SINGKAT — satu kalimat tajam per error, BUKAN paragraf penjelasan ala tutor.
- TIDAK ADA kolom/baris "Catatan Indonesia" di MANAPUN — baik di tabel koreksi (sudah hilang sejak C1) maupun di tabel BOW (baru hilang total di C2). Tabel BOW C2 hanya 2 kolom.
- Fallback kalau user stuck: tetap 100% English, tapi dibuat ringkas (paraphrase singkat/pilihan jawaban, tanpa penjelasan panjang).

### B. Trigger & Mekanisme Respons
- LANGKAH 1 berjalan otomatis begitu prompt dikirim (greeting + BOW + Writing Challenge dalam 1 response).
- LANGKAH 2 berjalan otomatis setelah user mengirim jawaban Writing Challenge.
- LANGKAH 3 (Speaking Mode) HANYA berjalan setelah user secara eksplisit mengetik "Let's start speaking!" sambil mode suara ChatGPT aktif.

### C. Box of Words (Wajib 15 Kata, Tabel 2 Kolom SAJA)
- Kolom: Kosakata + phonetic UK (`/ /`) | English Definition. TIDAK ADA kolom ketiga.
- Komposisi: 4-5 idiom retoris/native (bisa dimanipulasi untuk efek), 3-4 near-synonym dengan nuansa konotatif, 3-4 verbs/adjectives retoris, 2-3 discourse marker percakapan native, 1-2 fixed expression litotes/understatement.
- WAJIB cross-check terhadap seluruh BOW A1–C1 yang sudah ada — tidak boleh ada kata identik, hindari sinonim yang terlalu dekat.
- **🔂 Vocab Refresh (WAJIB mulai Day 2, sama seperti B2 dan C1):** Langkah 2 (Analisa BOW) harus menyinggung balik 1-2 kata dari BOW Day N-1 lewat satu kalimat singkat — BOW C2 (idiom retoris yang bisa dimanipulasi, litotes, near-synonym konotatif) adalah jenis kosakata paling cepat luruh tanpa repetisi karena frekuensinya rendah di percakapan sehari-hari, sehingga refresh dijaga tetap di Day 2 (bukan dimundurkan), bukan dipercepat lagi — pada titik ini retensi sudah dibantu oleh tingkat keterlibatan/elaborasi makna yang tinggi di level Mastery, bukan lagi murni oleh jadwal pengulangan.

### D. Writing Challenge
- Mode Cerita: 8-10 kalimat, minimal 5 kata BOW + minimal 1 momen craft retoris (ironi/understatement/fronting) yang disengaja, grammar/device utama Day ini WAJIB muncul.
- Mode Kilat: 5 kalimat (1 per kata BOW pilihan user), bergaya retoris, grammar/device utama Day ini WAJIB muncul.
- Instruksi task: Full English, ringkas.

### E. Koreksi 8 Langkah (Metodologi)

| Langkah | Isi | Bahasa |
|---|---|---|
| 0. Self-Check Pertama (mulai Day 1, khusus C1 & C2) | Tandai lokasi + jenis SATU pola error paling signifikan (kalau ada) tanpa beri jawaban, tunggu respons user, baru lanjut ke Langkah 1 | Full English, ringkas |
| 1. Koreksi Writing | Tabel Kalimat Asli \| Kalimat Benar \| Why (SATU kalimat) | Full English, TANPA kolom Catatan Indonesia |
| 2. Analisa BOW | ✅/⚠️ per kata + contoh kalimat ringkas. **Mulai Day 2:** + 🔂 Vocab Refresh | Full English |
| 3. Analisa CEFR | Evaluasi + 1-2 saran mempertahankan Mastery | Full English, ringkas |
| 4. 5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph | Tabel pembanding + paragraf diperkaya dengan momen craft | Full English, tanpa translation |
| 5. Discourse Markers | Cek + saran 2-3 discourse marker (akademik/native) | Full English |
| 6. Craft & Lexical Chunks | 2–3 highly nuanced fixed expressions, rhetorical moves, or near-synonym contrasts native Mastery-level speakers deploy in this context. Identify any in the user's writing (✅). If none, show one with a single sharp note on *why* it elevates register or rhetorical impact — no over-explanation, no hedging. | Full English |
| 7. Register/Formality Check | Flag any register slippage: nominalisation overuse, missing pragmatic hedges, inappropriate directness, or tone mismatch. Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent. |
| 8. Speaking Challenge | 3 pertanyaan topik terkait | Full English, tanpa translation |

**Research basis for Step 6:** *Lexical Approach* (Lewis, 1993) + Nattinger & DeCarrico (1992) on prefabricated language — at C2 Mastery level, the defining characteristic of native-like production is command of formulaic language: proverbs, rhetorical idioms, and near-native chunks that signal cultural fluency, not just grammatical accuracy. Step 6 makes this explicit where competitors stop at grammar correction.

**🔎 Self-Check Pertama (WAJIB mulai Day 1, khusus C1 & C2):** sebelum menampilkan tabel Koreksi Writing (Langkah 1), identifikasi SATU pola error paling signifikan di tulisan user (kalau ada). Tandai HANYA lokasi + jenis errornya dalam SATU kalimat tajam, tanpa memberi jawaban langsung — contoh: "Quick one first — sentence 3 has an inversion order slip. Want to try fixing it, or should I just show you?" Tunggu respons user (baik berupa percobaan perbaikan maupun permintaan jawaban langsung), BARU lanjutkan ke Langkah 1 yang tetap menampilkan direct feedback untuk SEMUA kalimat seperti biasa — sub-langkah ini menambah satu kesempatan self-correction di awal, bukan mengganti direct feedback yang sudah ada. Kalau tulisan user sudah ≥95% benar atau tidak ada pola error yang menonjol, lewati langkah ini dan langsung ke Langkah 1.

### F. Skeleton Dokumen per Day (6 Sub-Bagian, Urutan Tetap)
1. 📚 Detail Materi (BOW 2 kolom + grammar/device + kontras vs C1/B2 + konteks)
2. ✅ Detail Task (Mode Cerita + Mode Kilat + Speaking Challenge)
3. 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi (8 Langkah)
4. 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara
5. 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)
6. 🔗 PROMPT — Day X (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

### G. Penomoran Day & Daftar Topik
- Day 1-5: rhetorical device inti C2 paling fundamental (Rhetorical Fronting, Litotes, Idiom Manipulation, Near-Synonym Precision, Parallelism/Anaphora).
- Day 6-9: device pendukung (Hyperbole/Register-Shifting, Hedging-Boosting Continuum, Native Discourse Markers, Literary Tense Shifts).
- Day 10-14: kombinasi device + topik domain baru (persuasi, identitas multibahasa, ritual ucapan, sosiolinguistik), termasuk 1 bridge topic (Day 10, AI/Imajinasi Sastra).
- Day 15-21: kombinasi device lanjutan, topik baru sepenuhnya (filosofi keheningan, komedi, retorika hukum, etika persuasi, puisi, permintaan maaf publik, folklore).
- Day 22-29: kombinasi device campuran, 1 bridge topic lanjutan (Day 22, Climate Grief).
- Day 30: sintesis seluruh device C2 dalam 1 topik (The Last Lecture).
- Day 31: Final Capstone Assessment — BUKAN placement test ke level selanjutnya (C2 adalah level tertinggi CEFR), tapi konfirmasi penguasaan Mastery secara menyeluruh.

### H. Final Capstone Assessment (Day 31)

| Komponen | Detail |
|---|---|
| Format | Writing (1 esai bergaya bebas — bisa pidato, esai persuasif, atau narasi kreatif, 200-250 kata) + Speaking (3 pertanyaan reflektif yang menuntut craft, bukan hanya jawaban benar) |
| Grammar/device yang diuji | Seluruh rhetorical device C2 Day 1-30 (fronting, litotes, idiom manipulation, near-synonym precision, parallelism, dll) |
| Bahasa | Full English, gaya native, tanpa translation atau fallback Bahasa Indonesia dalam bentuk apapun |
| Kriteria penilaian | BUKAN "kelulusan ke level berikutnya" (tidak ada di atas C2) — penilaian fokus ke konsistensi craft, ketepatan nada budaya, dan kefasihan spontan setingkat penutur asli terdidik |
| Rekomendasi lanjutan | Setelah Day 31, user diarahkan ke Modul Khusus — English For Professionals (lihat `PRD_USER.md` §4.8) untuk pendalaman domain spesifik, bukan ke "level CEFR" baru |

---

## 📚 MATERI 30 TOPIK + FINAL CAPSTONE

---

### DAY 1 — Speeches That Changed Minds: The Craft of Rhetoric

#### 1. 📚 Detail Materi

**Box of Words (15 kata):**

| Kosakata | English Definition |
|---|---|
| resonate /ˈrez.ən.eɪt/ | to produce a strong feeling of shared emotion or belief, especially because of a personal connection |
| galvanize /ˈgæl.vən.aɪz/ | to shock or excite someone into taking action |
| evocative /ɪˈvɒk.ə.tɪv/ | bringing strong images, memories, or feelings to mind |
| visceral /ˈvɪs.ər.əl/ | relating to deep, instinctive feelings rather than reasoned thought |
| a rallying cry | a phrase or idea used to inspire a group to unite and take action |
| strike a chord | to say or do something that produces a strong, sympathetic reaction in people |
| eloquence /ˈel.ə.kwəns/ | fluent, persuasive, and naturally compelling speaking or writing |
| a turn of phrase | a particular way of saying something, especially a clever or memorable one |
| captivate /ˈkæp.tɪ.veɪt/ | to attract and hold the attention of someone completely |
| the gravity of | the seriousness or solemn importance of a situation |
| in no uncertain terms | said clearly and forcefully, leaving no room for doubt |
| crescendo /krɪˈʃen.dəʊ/ | a steady increase in intensity, force, or volume building to a climax |
| unequivocally /ˌʌn.ɪˈkwɪv.ə.kəl.i/ | in a way that leaves no doubt at all |
| command (verb) /kəˈmɑːnd/ | to deserve and get a particular reaction, such as attention or respect |
| a clarion call | a clear, strong call for people to do something, especially to take action |

**Grammar/Rhetorical Device: Rhetorical Fronting & Inversion**

Di C1, kamu belajar *Inverted Conditionals* (Had I known..., Were it not for...) — fungsinya FORMALITAS, mengganti "if" di teks resmi/akademik. Di C2, fronting dan inversion dipakai untuk fungsi yang sama sekali berbeda: **craft naratif/persuasif yang disengaja**. Ini bukan struktur yang "lebih sulit" — ini pilihan gaya yang dipakai penulis pidato, jurnalis, dan novelis untuk menciptakan efek dramatis dan ritme.

Tiga pola utama:

1. **Such + be + subject + that...** — menekankan intensitas suatu hal lalu menjelaskan akibatnya.
   - *Such was the power of her closing line that the entire hall fell silent.*
2. **So + adjective + be + subject + that...** — varian dengan adjective di depan untuk penekanan kualitas tertentu.
   - *So profound was the impact of his words that policymakers changed course within a week.*
3. **Gone are the days when...** — menandai kontras dramatis antara masa lalu dan sekarang, sering dipakai untuk membuka atau menutup argumen.
   - *Gone are the days when a single speech could unite an entire nation overnight.*

**Kontras fungsi (bukan sekadar tingkat kesulitan):**

| Level | Struktur | Fungsi |
|---|---|---|
| B2 | Negative adverbial inversion (Never have I..., Rarely does...) | Penekanan gramatikal, menunjukkan kontrol struktur |
| C1 | Inverted conditionals (Had I..., Were it not for...) | Formalitas register, menggantikan "if" di teks resmi |
| C2 | Rhetorical fronting (Such was..., So + adj + was..., Gone are the days when...) | Craft naratif yang DISENGAJA untuk efek dramatis — dipakai untuk persuasi, narasi, dan momen klimaks dalam pidato/tulisan |

**Konteks penggunaan:** Pidato politik dan kenegaraan, TED Talks, jurnalisme naratif, esai persuasif, dan momen "punchline" dalam tulisan opini — kapan pun penulis ingin menandai bahwa kalimat ini adalah titik penekanan, bukan informasi biasa.

---

#### 2. ✅ Detail Task

**Writing Challenge**

📖 **Mode Cerita** (8-10 kalimat): Write about a speech, real or imagined, that left a lasting impression on you or on history. Use at least 5 words from the Box of Words and at least one deliberate moment of rhetorical fronting (Such was.../So + adj + was.../Gone are the days when...).

⚡ **Mode Kilat** (5 kalimat): Pick 5 words from the Box of Words. Write one rhetorically-charged sentence per word, using the fronting/inversion pattern from today's grammar focus.

**Speaking Challenge** (3 pertanyaan, ditampilkan setelah koreksi writing):
1. What is the most evocative speech or piece of writing you've ever encountered — and why did it resonate with you?
2. Some say eloquence is a skill that can be learned, while others believe it's innate. Where do you stand?
3. If you had to deliver a single rallying cry to galvanize people on an issue you care about, what would it be?

---

#### 3. 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi 8 Langkah

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why (satu kalimat tajam). Kalimat sudah tepat ditandai ✅, Why diisi "—".

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — Cek setiap kata BOW yang dipakai user: ✅ tepat / ⚠️ belum tepat + contoh kalimat natural pengganti, ringkas, langsung.

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Evaluasi singkat: apa yang sudah kuat di tulisan user (craft, ritme, ketepatan device) + 1-2 saran untuk mempertahankan Mastery, bukan "naik level".

4️⃣ **5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph** — Tabel ringkas What/Why/Where/When/Who/How dari tulisan user, lalu versi "Enriched Paragraph" yang sama isinya tapi dengan minimal satu momen rhetorical fronting tambahan, full English.

5️⃣ **Discourse Markers** — Cek pemakaian. Kalau belum ada, sarankan 2-3 (akademik: *insofar as, by the same token* / native: *for what it's worth, if anything*) + contoh kalimat.

6️⃣ **Craft & Lexical Chunks** — 2–3 high-register lexical chunks native Mastery-level speakers use for rhetoric and speeches (e.g. **strike a chord**, **a rallying cry**, **leave a lasting impression**). Identify any in user's writing (✅). If none, suggest one with a single sharp note on why it elevates register — one sentence, no over-explanation.

7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent throughout.

8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — tampilkan 3 pertanyaan di atas.

**Contoh koreksi (ilustrasi gaya, bukan template kaku):**

| Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why |
|---|---|---|
| It was such a powerful speech that everyone got silent. | Such was the power of the speech that the room fell silent. | Fronting "such" sharpens the climax — "it was such a" reads flat by comparison. |
| The speaker have a great eloquence. | The speaker possessed remarkable eloquence. | Subject-verb agreement; "possessed" suits the register better than "have." |

---

#### 4. 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

- Tone: native-direct, ringkas, percaya pada otonomi user. Tidak menjelaskan ulang teori dasar grammar yang sudah dikuasai di C1.
- Error umum di topik ini: pakai fronting tanpa benar-benar menempatkannya di titik klimaks (sehingga efeknya hilang); subject-verb mismatch dalam struktur inversion ("Such was the speeches" → seharusnya "speeches were").
- Template pujian: singkat, spesifik ke craft — contoh: "That fronting in your third sentence landed exactly where it should — nice instinct for pacing."
- Saran mempertahankan Mastery: dorong user mencoba memakai fronting di TITIK KLIMAKS kalimat, bukan di awal sembarangan — efeknya baru terasa kalau ditempatkan tepat.

---

#### 5. 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

- Trigger: user mengetik "Let's start speaking!" dengan mode suara aktif.
- Ajukan 3 pertanyaan Speaking Challenge satu per satu, full English, langsung tanpa basa-basi.
- Kalau user lancar: tambahkan pertanyaan lanjutan yang menaikkan abstraksi — misalnya "Can you give me an example of a rallying cry that backfired instead of galvanizing support?"
- Kalau user macet: beri paraphrase singkat atau pilihan jawaban, full English, tanpa penjelasan panjang.
- Pujian hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan ringkas.

---

#### 6. 🔗 PROMPT — Day 1 (Copy-Paste ke ChatGPT)

```
Topik: Speeches That Changed Minds: The Craft of Rhetoric
Panggil aku [PANGGILAN] [NAMA].
Level bahasa Inggrisku: C2 (Mastery/Proficient).
Kamu Kak Ara, personal AI Coach kamu, dari Inggrisin Yuk. Tugasmu membimbingku belajar vocab lewat writing dan speaking di Level C2 (Mastery).

Gaya bahasa: sopan, ramah, humble (rendah hati — tidak menggurui), tapi singkat, langsung, dan native-like — anggap aku sudah fasih, jangan jelaskan ulang teori dasar grammar.
Gunakan Full English untuk SEMUA penjelasan, instruksi, koreksi, dan feedback — TANPA terjemahan atau catatan Bahasa Indonesia dalam bentuk apapun, termasuk di tabel Box of Words (tidak ada kolom Bahasa Indonesia sama sekali).
Koreksi dibuat SINGKAT dan TAJAM — satu kalimat per error, gaya native menegur native.
Tampilkan phonetic symbol UK setelah setiap kosakata dalam tanda / /.

LANGKAH 1 — Sapa singkat ("Hi! It's Kak Ara from Inggrisin Yuk 👋"), lalu tampilkan:
📦 Box of Words — Use EXACTLY these 15 words (do not add or substitute any):
resonate, galvanize, evocative, visceral, a rallying cry, strike a chord, eloquence, a turn of phrase, captivate, the gravity of, in no uncertain terms, crescendo, unequivocally, command, a clarion call
Display in a 2-column table only: Kosakata+phonetic | English Definition. Add UK phonetics where not shown.
✍️ Writing Challenge — Mode Cerita (8-10 kalimat tentang a speech that left a lasting impression, pakai 5 kata BOW + grammar fronting hari ini) dan Mode Kilat (5 kalimat, 1 per kata BOW, pakai fronting/inversion).
Grammar fokus hari ini: Rhetorical Fronting & Inversion (Such was... that / So + adj + was... that / Gone are the days when...) — jelaskan singkat bedanya dengan inverted conditionals C1 (formalitas vs craft naratif).

LANGKAH 2 — Setelah aku kirim tulisan, kalau ada SATU pola error paling signifikan (terutama soal urutan inversi setelah fronting, misalnya subjek-verba yang tidak terbalik dengan benar setelah "Such was..." atau "Gone are the days..."), tandai dulu HANYA lokasi + jenis errornya dalam satu kalimat tajam tanpa kasih jawaban (Self-Check Pertama), tunggu responsku. Kalau tulisanku sudah ≥95% benar, lewati langsung. Lalu jalankan Koreksi 8 Langkah: (1) Koreksi Writing (tabel Kalimat Asli | Kalimat Benar | Why singkat, tanpa kolom Bahasa Indonesia), (2) Analisa BOW, (3) Analisa CEFR (saran mempertahankan Mastery), (4) 5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph, (5) Discourse Markers, (6) Craft & Lexical Chunks — 2-3 high-register lexical chunks native speakers use for rhetoric/speeches (e.g. **strike a chord**, **a rallying cry**, **leave a lasting impression**); check if used naturally (✅); suggest one to try, (7) Register/Formality Check — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent, (8) Speaking Challenge (3 pertanyaan tentang eloquence, rallying cries, dan speeches yang membekas). If my writing is blank or not in English, ask me to write first.

LANGKAH 3 — Kalau aku aktifkan mode suara dan ketik "Let's start speaking!", ajukan Speaking Challenge satu per satu, full English, koreksi singkat dan langsung.
```

---

### DAY 2 — The Art of Understatement: Saying Less to Mean More

#### 1. 📚 Detail Materi

**Box of Words (15 kata):**

| Kosakata | English Definition |
|---|---|
| understatement /ˈʌn.də.steɪt.mənt/ | a statement that describes something in a way that makes it seem less important, serious, or impressive than it really is |
| no mean feat | something that is difficult and deserves admiration, despite being described modestly |
| not exactly | used ironically to mean the opposite of what follows |
| far from | used to emphasize that something is the opposite of what is described |
| leave something to be desired | to be not as good as it should be |
| tongue-in-cheek /ˌtʌŋ ɪn ˈtʃiːk/ | said or done in a way that is not meant to be taken seriously, though it may sound serious |
| downplay /ˌdaʊnˈpleɪ/ | to make something seem less important than it really is |
| diplomatic /ˌdɪp.ləˈmæt.ɪk/ | tactful in dealing with sensitive matters or people |
| a backhanded compliment | a remark that seems to be a compliment but could also be an insult |
| wry /raɪ/ | showing dry, slightly mocking humor |
| self-deprecating /ˌself ˈdep.rɪ.keɪ.tɪŋ/ | tending to make modest or critical statements about oneself, often humorously |
| understated /ˌʌn.dəˈsteɪ.tɪd/ | (of something impressive) presented or expressed in a subtle, controlled way |
| mild (ironic use) /maɪld/ | used ironically to soften a description of something serious — e.g. "a mild inconvenience" for something disastrous |
| par for the course | something that is normal or expected, especially something undesirable |
| not without its challenges | used to acknowledge difficulty while minimizing how it sounds |

**Grammar/Rhetorical Device: Litotes & Rhetorical Understatement**

Di B2, kamu belajar *hedging* — melembutkan KEPASTIAN (might, perhaps). Di C1, kamu belajar spektrum modal epistemic — melembutkan KEMUNGKINAN secara presisi (might well, could conceivably). Di C2, litotes melembutkan sesuatu yang berbeda lagi: **EVALUASI dan EMOSI**, lewat negasi + kata ringan untuk menyiratkan sesuatu yang sebenarnya lebih kuat. Ini adalah ciri khas tact, ironi, dan diplomasi penutur asli.

Pola utama:

1. **not + (adjective/adverb opposite)** — menyiratkan sesuatu lebih kuat dari kata yang dipakai.
   - *The negotiations were not exactly smooth.* (= they were tense, difficult)
2. **far from + (adjective/noun)** — menegaskan jarak dari kondisi ideal.
   - *The results were far from satisfactory.* (= they were quite bad)
3. **no mean feat / not without its challenges** — frasa fixed yang mengakui kesulitan sambil terdengar santai.
   - *Negotiating that treaty without a single walkout was no mean feat.*

**Kontras fungsi (bukan sekadar tingkat kesulitan):**

| Level | Struktur | Fungsi |
|---|---|---|
| B2 | Hedging (might, perhaps, it seems that) | Melembutkan KEPASTIAN — penulis belum yakin |
| C1 | Epistemic modal spectrum (might well, could conceivably) | Melembutkan KEMUNGKINAN secara presisi — penulis yakin tapi memilih nuansa probabilitas tertentu |
| C2 | Litotes & understatement (not exactly, far from, no mean feat) | Melembutkan EVALUASI/EMOSI lewat ironi — penulis tahu persis seberapa kuat sesuatu, tapi memilih menyiratkannya secara halus untuk efek tact atau humor |

**Konteks penggunaan:** Percakapan diplomatik, review/kritik yang sopan tapi jujur, humor self-deprecating, jurnalisme bernada ironis, dan situasi sosial di mana mengatakan sesuatu secara langsung dianggap kurang sopan atau kurang elegan.

---

#### 2. ✅ Detail Task

**Writing Challenge**

📖 **Mode Cerita** (8-10 kalimat): Write about a situation — a project, a trip, an event — that did not go as planned, but describe it using understatement and litotes rather than direct complaint. Use at least 5 words from the Box of Words and at least one deliberate litotes construction (not exactly / far from / no mean feat).

⚡ **Mode Kilat** (5 kalimat): Pick 5 words from the Box of Words. Write one ironically understated sentence per word.

**Speaking Challenge** (3 pertanyaan, ditampilkan setelah koreksi writing):
1. Tell me about a time something went far from perfectly — but try to describe it the way a diplomat would.
2. Do you think understatement is a sign of politeness, or can it sometimes be a way of avoiding honesty?
3. Give me a backhanded compliment about something you secretly don't like — keep it tongue-in-cheek.

---

#### 3. 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi 8 Langkah

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why (satu kalimat tajam). Kalimat sudah tepat ditandai ✅, Why diisi "—".

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — Cek setiap kata BOW yang dipakai user: ✅ tepat / ⚠️ belum tepat + contoh kalimat natural pengganti, ringkas, langsung. Sertakan juga 1 kalimat singkat yang menyegarkan kembali 1-2 kata dari Box of Words Day 1 (vocab refresh).

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Evaluasi singkat: apakah litotes yang dipakai user benar-benar terdengar ironis/diplomatik atau malah terbaca sebagai kalimat negatif biasa + 1-2 saran mempertahankan Mastery.

4️⃣ **5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph** — Tabel ringkas What/Why/Where/When/Who/How dari tulisan user, lalu "Enriched Paragraph" versi yang sama dengan tambahan minimal satu litotes baru, full English.

5️⃣ **Discourse Markers** — Cek pemakaian. Kalau belum ada, sarankan 2-3 (akademik: *notwithstanding, by the same token* / native: *if anything, at the end of the day*) + contoh kalimat.

6️⃣ **Craft & Lexical Chunks** — 2–3 lexical chunks native Mastery-level speakers use for understatement and diplomacy (e.g. **not exactly**, **a backhanded compliment**, **tongue-in-cheek**). Identify any in user's writing (✅). If none, suggest one with a single sharp note on why it sharpens the rhetorical effect — one sentence, no over-explanation.

7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent throughout.

8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — tampilkan 3 pertanyaan di atas.

**Contoh koreksi (ilustrasi gaya, bukan template kaku):**

| Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why |
|---|---|---|
| The trip was very bad and everything went wrong. | The trip was far from smooth, to put it mildly. | Litotes lands the same meaning with more tact — "very bad" reads blunt, not ironic. |
| It was no mean feats to finish on time. | It was no mean feat to finish on time. | "No mean feat" is a fixed singular phrase — never pluralized. |

---

#### 4. 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

- Tone: native-direct, ringkas. Tidak menjelaskan ulang konsep hedging/modal dari level sebelumnya.
- Error umum di topik ini: memakai litotes tapi konteksnya tetap terdengar sebagai komplain langsung (kehilangan efek ironis); menyalahgunakan "not exactly" untuk hal yang benar-benar netral, bukan untuk menyiratkan sesuatu yang lebih kuat.
- Template pujian: spesifik ke ketepatan nada — contoh: "That backhanded compliment was perfectly placed — dry, controlled, and unmistakably ironic."
- Saran mempertahankan Mastery: dorong user mencoba litotes dalam konteks SOSIAL nyata (memberi kritik halus ke teman/kolega) supaya fungsinya terasa, bukan cuma latihan kalimat lepas.

---

#### 5. 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

- Trigger: user mengetik "Let's start speaking!" dengan mode suara aktif.
- Ajukan 3 pertanyaan Speaking Challenge satu per satu, full English, langsung tanpa basa-basi.
- Kalau user lancar: tambahkan pertanyaan lanjutan yang menantang nuansa lebih jauh — misalnya "Can you turn that into a backhanded compliment instead?"
- Kalau user macet: beri paraphrase singkat atau pilihan jawaban, full English, tanpa penjelasan panjang.
- Pujian hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan ringkas.

---

### DAY 3 — Wit, Irony & the Ethics of Humor

#### 1. 📚 Detail Materi

**Box of Words (15 kata):**

| Kosakata | English Definition |
|---|---|
| wit /wɪt/ | the capacity for quick, inventive verbal humor |
| deadpan /ˈded.pæn/ | deliberately impassive or expressionless, especially as a comic technique |
| a pun /pʌn/ | a joke that exploits the different possible meanings of a word, or words that sound alike |
| double entendre /ˌduː.bəl ɒnˈtɒn.drə/ | a word or phrase open to two interpretations, one of which is typically risqué or irreverent |
| quip /kwɪp/ | a witty, often sarcastic, remark |
| wisecrack /ˈwaɪz.kræk/ | a clever, sharp remark made on the spur of the moment |
| facetious /fəˈsiː.ʃəs/ | treating a serious subject with deliberately inappropriate humor |
| a play on words | wordplay that exploits multiple meanings or similar sounds for comic effect |
| cross the line | to go beyond what is acceptable, especially regarding humor or behavior |
| below the belt | unfair or unnecessarily cruel, especially in a joke or criticism |
| in jest | said or done as a joke, not seriously |
| punchline | the final phrase of a joke that delivers the comic payoff |
| a running gag | a joke or reference repeated throughout a piece for cumulative comic effect |
| comic timing | the skill of saying or doing something funny at exactly the right moment |
| it's all fun and games until... | used to mark the point at which humor stops being harmless and becomes a problem |

**Grammar/Rhetorical Device: Idiom Manipulation & Wordplay**

At earlier levels, idioms are learned and used according to their fixed, standard meaning. At C2, native speakers routinely *manipulate* a known idiom — subverting it, extending it, or taking it literally — for comic or ironic effect. This is not a new structure; it's a skill that only works once the original idiom is already fully mastered. Manipulating an idiom you don't actually know just reads as an error, not a joke.

Three manipulation patterns:

1. **Subversion** — negating or twisting the expected ending of a familiar idiom.
   - *Curiosity killed the cat — and, frankly, the cat had it coming.*
2. **Extension** — continuing a fixed idiom into unexpected territory.
   - *Don't count your chickens before they hatch — or, in this office, before they unionize.*
3. **Literalization** — taking a figurative idiom literally for comic effect.
   - *He said he'd give his right arm for the promotion. HR took him at his word.*

**Kontras fungsi (bukan sekadar tingkat kesulitan):**

| Level | Idiom Usage | Fungsi |
|---|---|---|
| B1–B2 | Fixed idioms used per standard meaning (break the ice, hit the nail on the head) | Conversational fluency marker — sounding less textbook |
| C1 | Formal/institutional idioms (a far cry from, by the same token, to all intents and purposes) | Register marker — signals formal, academic, or professional writing |
| C2 | Idiom manipulation (subversion, extension, literalization) | Deliberate comic/ironic craft — requires complete mastery of the original idiom to bend it convincingly |

**Konteks penggunaan:** Stand-up comedy, satirical writing, witty conversation among native speakers, comedic essays, banter, and any context where a listener's recognition of the *original* idiom is the whole point of the joke.

---

#### 2. ✅ Detail Task

**Writing Challenge**

📖 **Mode Cerita** (8-10 kalimat): Write about a moment — real or invented — where someone's humor either landed perfectly or badly misfired. Use at least 5 words from the Box of Words and at least one deliberate idiom manipulation (subversion, extension, or literalization).

⚡ **Mode Kilat** (5 kalimat): Pick 5 words from the Box of Words. Write one sentence per word that manipulates a well-known idiom for comic or ironic effect.

**Speaking Challenge** (3 pertanyaan, ditampilkan setelah koreksi writing):
1. What's the wittiest comeback or quip you've ever heard — or wished you'd thought of in the moment?
2. Where do you personally draw the line between a joke that's in jest and one that's gone below the belt?
3. Take a well-known idiom and manipulate it — subvert it, extend it, or take it literally — to make it funny.

---

#### 3. 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi 8 Langkah

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why (satu kalimat tajam). Kalimat sudah tepat ditandai ✅, Why diisi "—".

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — Cek setiap kata BOW yang dipakai user: ✅ tepat / ⚠️ belum tepat + contoh kalimat natural pengganti, ringkas, langsung. Sertakan juga 1 kalimat singkat yang menyegarkan kembali 1-2 kata dari Box of Words Day 2 (vocab refresh).

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Evaluasi singkat: apakah idiom yang dimanipulasi user benar-benar landed sebagai humor/ironi, atau malah terbaca sebagai error grammar biasa + 1-2 saran mempertahankan Mastery.

4️⃣ **5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph** — Tabel ringkas What/Why/Where/When/Who/How dari tulisan user, lalu "Enriched Paragraph" versi yang sama dengan tambahan minimal satu idiom manipulation baru, full English.

5️⃣ **Discourse Markers** — Cek pemakaian. Kalau belum ada, sarankan 2-3 (akademik: *notwithstanding, that said* / native: *mind you, if anything*) + contoh kalimat.

6️⃣ **Craft & Lexical Chunks** — 2–3 lexical chunks native Mastery-level speakers use for humor and wit (e.g. **a running gag**, **below the belt**, **comic timing**). Identify any in user's writing (✅). If none, suggest one with a single sharp note on why it sharpens the comic effect — one sentence, no over-explanation.

7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent throughout.

8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — tampilkan 3 pertanyaan di atas.

**Contoh koreksi (ilustrasi gaya, bukan template kaku):**

| Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why |
|---|---|---|
| Curiosity kill the cat, but the cat deserve it. | Curiosity killed the cat — and, frankly, the cat had it coming. | Subject-verb agreement aside, the manipulated ending lands sharper with "had it coming" than "deserve it." |
| He make a joke that was very below the belt. | He made a joke that was well below the belt. | "Well below the belt" intensifies more naturally than "very" with this idiom. |

---

#### 4. 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

- Tone: native-direct, ringkas. Tidak menjelaskan ulang apa itu idiom — anggap user sudah paham idiom standar dari level sebelumnya.
- Error umum di topik ini: memanipulasi idiom tanpa benar-benar menguasai bentuk aslinya (sehingga terdengar salah, bukan lucu); humor yang terlalu below the belt untuk konteks yang ditulis; kehilangan comic timing karena punchline diletakkan di tengah kalimat, bukan di akhir.
- Template pujian: spesifik ke craft — contoh: "That idiom subversion landed exactly where the punchline should — nice instinct for timing."
- Saran mempertahankan Mastery: dorong user mencoba memanipulasi idiom yang BENAR-BENAR mereka kenal luar dalam — manipulasi idiom yang masih asing biasanya gagal landed.

---

#### 5. 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

- Trigger: user mengetik "Let's start speaking!" dengan mode suara aktif.
- Ajukan 3 pertanyaan Speaking Challenge satu per satu, full English, langsung tanpa basa-basi.
- Kalau user lancar: tambahkan pertanyaan lanjutan yang menantang nuansa lebih jauh — misalnya "Can you think of a joke that crossed the line for some people but not for others? What made the difference?"
- Kalau user macet: beri paraphrase singkat atau pilihan jawaban, full English, tanpa penjelasan panjang.
- Pujian hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan ringkas.

---

### DAY 4 — Untranslatable Words & the Limits of Language

#### 1. 📚 Detail Materi

**Box of Words (15 kata):**

| Kosakata | English Definition |
|---|---|
| schadenfreude /ˈʃɑː.dən.frɔɪ.də/ | (German loanword) pleasure derived from another person's misfortune |
| hiraeth /ˈhɪə.raɪθ/ | (Welsh loanword) a deep, wistful longing for a home or time that may no longer exist |
| l'esprit de l'escalier /lɛs.priː də lɛs.kæl.jeɪ/ | (French) the witty retort that comes to mind only after the moment to use it has passed |
| fernweh /ˈfɛrn.veɪ/ | (German loanword) a longing for distant places one has never been |
| sonder /ˈsɒn.dər/ | the realization that every passerby is living a life as vivid and complex as one's own |
| mono no aware /ˌmɒn.oʊ noʊ əˈwɑːr.eɪ/ | (Japanese) a wistful awareness of the impermanence of things |
| wistful /ˈwɪst.fəl/ | having or showing a feeling of vague or regretful longing |
| lost in translation | meaning or nuance that disappears when something is rendered into another language |
| coin a word/phrase | to invent a new word or expression |
| defies translation | used of a word or concept so culturally specific that no single equivalent exists elsewhere |
| connotation /ˌkɒn.əˈteɪ.ʃən/ | an idea or feeling a word invokes beyond its literal, dictionary meaning |
| semantically loaded | carrying strong additional emotional or cultural meaning beyond the literal definition |
| untranslatable /ˌʌn.trænzˈleɪ.tə.bəl/ | unable to be rendered into another language without losing essential meaning |
| a precise word for it | a fixed expression meaning exactly the right term that captures a nuance |
| get something across | to convey a meaning successfully, especially when it is hard to express |

**Grammar/Rhetorical Device: Nuanced Near-Synonym & Connotation Precision**

Untranslatable loanwords exist precisely because a language sometimes lacks a single word for a very specific cultural or emotional nuance. But within English itself, native speakers compensate for this constantly — not by inventing new words, but by choosing with extreme precision among near-synonyms that already exist, based on **connotation**, not denotation. Mastery here means selecting the exact word whose emotional shade matches your intent, not just a word that's technically correct.

Three near-synonym sets that illustrate the device:

1. **lonely** (painful, negative) vs. **solitary** (neutral, often chosen) vs. **alone** (purely factual).
   - *She wasn't lonely — she was solitary, and she'd chosen it that way.*
2. **thrifty** (positive — careful with money) vs. **frugal** (neutral-positive) vs. **stingy** (negative — unwilling to spend even when appropriate).
   - *He isn't stingy, he's just thrifty — there's a difference, and it matters to him.*
3. **assertive** (positive) vs. **pushy** (negative), describing near-identical behavior with opposite judgment built in.
   - *Call it assertive if you respect her; call it pushy if you don't — the behavior never changed, only the word.*

**Kontras fungsi (bukan sekadar tingkat kesulitan):**

| Level | Lexical Strategy | Fungsi |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | Nominalisation as a register strategy (implementation, accountability) | Chooses FORMALITY — the same idea named more or less formally |
| C2 | Near-synonym & connotation precision (lonely/solitary/alone) | Chooses EMOTIONAL JUDGMENT — near-identical denotation, opposite or different built-in evaluation |

**Konteks penggunaan:** Literary translation, memoir and emotionally precise writing, conflict-sensitive conversations where word choice can escalate or de-escalate tension, branding and copywriting where a single word carries reputational risk.

---

#### 2. ✅ Detail Task

**Writing Challenge**

📖 **Mode Cerita** (8-10 kalimat): Write about a feeling or experience you've had that English struggles to capture precisely — and try to get it across anyway, using the most emotionally exact words you can find. Use at least 5 words from the Box of Words and deliberately contrast at least one pair of near-synonyms for their connotation.

⚡ **Mode Kilat** (5 kalimat): Pick 5 words from the Box of Words. Write one sentence per word that shows its precise emotional shade, ideally contrasted against a near-synonym.

**Speaking Challenge** (3 pertanyaan, ditampilkan setelah koreksi writing):
1. Is there a feeling you've experienced that you think English simply doesn't have the right word for? Try to describe it.
2. Give me two near-synonyms in English that mean almost the same thing but carry opposite judgments — like "assertive" vs. "pushy."
3. Have you ever had a moment of l'esprit de l'escalier — thinking of the perfect comeback far too late? Tell me about it.

---

#### 3. 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi 8 Langkah

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why (satu kalimat tajam). Kalimat sudah tepat ditandai ✅, Why diisi "—".

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — Cek setiap kata BOW yang dipakai user: ✅ tepat / ⚠️ belum tepat + contoh kalimat natural pengganti, ringkas, langsung. Sertakan juga 1 kalimat singkat yang menyegarkan kembali 1-2 kata dari Box of Words Day 3 (vocab refresh).

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Evaluasi singkat: apakah near-synonym yang dipilih user benar-benar membawa konotasi yang dimaksud, atau dipilih sekadar karena "terdengar lebih canggih" + 1-2 saran mempertahankan Mastery.

4️⃣ **5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph** — Tabel ringkas What/Why/Where/When/Who/How dari tulisan user, lalu "Enriched Paragraph" versi yang sama dengan minimal satu near-synonym swap baru yang menunjukkan konotasi lebih presisi, full English.

5️⃣ **Discourse Markers** — Cek pemakaian. Kalau belum ada, sarankan 2-3 (akademik: *insofar as, by the same token* / native: *mind you, if anything*) + contoh kalimat.

6️⃣ **Craft & Lexical Chunks** — 2–3 lexical chunks native Mastery-level speakers use when discussing language and nuance (e.g. **lost in translation**, **a precise word for it**, **get something across**). Identify any in user's writing (✅). If none, suggest one with a single sharp note on why it sharpens precision — one sentence, no over-explanation.

7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent throughout.

8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — tampilkan 3 pertanyaan di atas.

**Contoh koreksi (ilustrasi gaya, bukan template kaku):**

| Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why |
|---|---|---|
| I felt very alone, like nobody understand me. | I felt a hiraeth-like ache, like something I couldn't quite name. | "Alone" flattens the feeling — the Box of Words exists precisely to avoid that flattening. |
| That word don't have direct translation in English. | That word defies translation into English. | "Defies translation" is the precise fixed expression; "don't have direct translation" reads as a literal calque. |

---

#### 4. 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

- Tone: native-direct, ringkas. Tidak menjelaskan ulang konsep sinonim dasar — anggap user sudah tahu near-synonyms BUKAN kata yang identik maknanya.
- Error umum di topik ini: memilih near-synonym yang "terdengar mewah" tanpa memperhatikan konotasinya benar-benar cocok (misalnya pakai "stingy" untuk menggambarkan diri sendiri secara positif); memakai loanword asing tanpa memahami nuansanya secara tepat.
- Template pujian: spesifik ke ketepatan konotasi — contoh: "Choosing 'solitary' instead of 'lonely' there completely changed the emotional register — that's exactly the kind of precision this Day is about."
- Saran mempertahankan Mastery: dorong user membuat daftar pribadi near-synonym yang sering tertukar dalam tulisan mereka sendiri, dan secara sadar memilih berdasarkan konotasi setiap kali menulis.

---

#### 5. 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

- Trigger: user mengetik "Let's start speaking!" dengan mode suara aktif.
- Ajukan 3 pertanyaan Speaking Challenge satu per satu, full English, langsung tanpa basa-basi.
- Kalau user lancar: tambahkan pertanyaan lanjutan — misalnya "Can you think of a word in your own language that you think English simply can't capture as precisely?"
- Kalau user macet: beri paraphrase singkat atau pilihan jawaban, full English, tanpa penjelasan panjang.
- Pujian hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan ringkas.

---

### DAY 5 — The Art of the Eulogy: Ceremonial Speech & Legacy

#### 1. 📚 Detail Materi

**Box of Words (15 kata):**

| Kosakata | English Definition |
|---|---|
| eulogy /ˈjuː.lə.dʒi/ | a speech or piece of writing that praises someone who has died |
| epitaph /ˈep.ɪ.tɑːf/ | a phrase or short text honoring a deceased person, often inscribed on a tombstone |
| in memoriam /ɪn məˈmɔːr.i.æm/ | a Latin phrase used to honor and remember someone who has died, typically in a dedication |
| in loving memory | a phrase used to dedicate something to someone who has died |
| larger than life | having a vivid, exuberant, or impressive personal quality that makes someone seem more than ordinary |
| leave one's mark | to have a lasting and noticeable effect or influence |
| a life well-lived | used to describe someone's life as full, meaningful, and admirable |
| pay tribute to | to publicly express respect and admiration for someone |
| solemn /ˈsɒl.əm/ | formal and serious, especially in a respectful way |
| poignant /ˈpɒɪ.njənt/ | evoking a keen sense of sadness or regret |
| irreplaceable /ˌɪr.ɪˈpleɪ.sə.bəl/ | too valuable or unique to be replaced by anyone or anything else |
| gone but not forgotten | used to say that, although someone has died, they will continue to be remembered |
| lay to rest | to bury a deceased person, often used as a gentler alternative to "bury" |
| the measure of a person | the true worth or character of someone, often revealed by how they lived or what they did |
| fondly remembered | described or thought of with affection and warmth, especially after death |

**Grammar/Rhetorical Device: Parallelism, Anaphora & Rhetorical Triads**

Ceremonial speech — eulogies, toasts, dedications — is governed by deliberate repetition of structure for rhythm and emotional weight, far beyond ordinary listing. This is the rhetorical engine behind why a well-written eulogy sounds different from a biography: it isn't just *what* is said, but how the structure itself carries the gravity.

Three patterns:

1. **Anaphora** — repeating the same opening word or phrase at the start of successive clauses.
   - *She taught us patience. She taught us humility. She taught us, above all, how to begin again.*
2. **Parallelism** — mirroring grammatical structure across clauses for balance and weight.
   - *Not how long she lived, but how fully she lived it.*
3. **Rhetorical triad** — grouping ideas in sets of three for rhythm and memorability.
   - *A mother, a mentor, and — to many of us — a friend.*

**Kontras fungsi (bukan sekadar tingkat kesulitan):**

| Level | Structure | Fungsi |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | Multi-clause embedding (subordinating ideas into one dense, complex sentence) | Compresses information for analytical density |
| C2 | Parallelism, anaphora & rhetorical triads (deliberate structural repetition across multiple clauses) | Builds rhythm, ritual gravity, and memorability — the hallmark of spoken ceremonial register |

**Konteks penggunaan:** Eulogies, wedding toasts, retirement speeches, graduation addresses, obituaries, and dedications — any context where the spoken or written word must carry the emotional weight of a milestone or a loss.

---

#### 2. ✅ Detail Task

**Writing Challenge**

📖 **Mode Cerita** (8-10 kalimat): Write a short eulogy or tribute for someone — real, fictional, or even a beloved pet or place — capturing what made them irreplaceable. Use at least 5 words from the Box of Words and at least one deliberate moment of anaphora, parallelism, or a rhetorical triad.

⚡ **Mode Kilat** (5 kalimat): Pick 5 words from the Box of Words. Write one solemn, tribute-style sentence per word.

**Speaking Challenge** (3 pertanyaan, ditampilkan setelah koreksi writing):
1. If you had to deliver a eulogy for someone who shaped who you are, what's the one quality you'd want people to remember most about them?
2. Why do you think ceremonial speeches — eulogies, toasts — so often rely on repetition and rhythm, rather than just stating facts plainly?
3. Try delivering a short rhetorical triad summing up someone you admire — three words or phrases, building to the strongest.

---

#### 3. 🔍 Detail Review & Koreksi 8 Langkah

1️⃣ **Koreksi Writing** — Tabel: Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why (satu kalimat tajam). Kalimat sudah tepat ditandai ✅, Why diisi "—".

2️⃣ **Analisa BOW** — Cek setiap kata BOW yang dipakai user: ✅ tepat / ⚠️ belum tepat + contoh kalimat natural pengganti, ringkas, langsung. Sertakan juga 1 kalimat singkat yang menyegarkan kembali 1-2 kata dari Box of Words Day 4 (vocab refresh).

3️⃣ **Analisa CEFR** — Evaluasi singkat: apakah parallelism/anaphora/triad yang dipakai user benar-benar terasa ritmis dan disengaja, atau hanya pengulangan kebetulan + 1-2 saran mempertahankan Mastery.

4️⃣ **5W+1H + Enriched Paragraph** — Tabel ringkas What/Why/Where/When/Who/How dari tulisan user, lalu "Enriched Paragraph" versi yang sama dengan tambahan minimal satu anaphora/triad baru, full English.

5️⃣ **Discourse Markers** — Cek pemakaian. Kalau belum ada, sarankan 2-3 (akademik: *by the same token, notwithstanding* / native: *mind you, if anything*) + contoh kalimat.

6️⃣ **Craft & Lexical Chunks** — 2–3 lexical chunks native Mastery-level speakers use for tributes and ceremonial speech (e.g. **leave one's mark**, **a life well-lived**, **gone but not forgotten**). Identify any in user's writing (✅). If none, suggest one with a single sharp note on why it elevates the register — one sentence, no over-explanation.

7️⃣ **Register/Formality Check** — Spot any register slippage (formal/colloquial, academic/journalistic, or pragmatic tone mismatch). Format: Original → More appropriate → Why (one sharp native-to-native note). ✅ skip if consistent throughout.

8️⃣ **Speaking Challenge** — tampilkan 3 pertanyaan di atas.

**Contoh koreksi (ilustrasi gaya, bukan template kaku):**

| Kalimat Asli | Kalimat yang Benar | Why |
|---|---|---|
| He was kind, he was funny, and he help everyone. | He was kind. He was funny. He helped everyone, without ever being asked. | Splitting into short anaphoric sentences carries far more ceremonial weight than one run-on clause. |
| She will be remember forever by everyone who knew her. | She will be fondly remembered by everyone who knew her. | Past participle needed after "be"; "fondly remembered" is also the precise ceremonial collocation. |

---

#### 4. 💬 Detail Feedback & Panduan Kak Ara

- Tone: native-direct, ringkas, tapi tetap menghormati kepekaan emosional topik ini — pujian tetap tulus tanpa terasa klinis.
- Error umum di topik ini: menumpuk terlalu banyak detail biografis tanpa struktur ritmis (membaca seperti CV, bukan eulogy); anaphora yang dipaksakan sehingga terasa kaku, bukan mengalir; triad yang isinya tidak naik intensitasnya (urutan datar, bukan klimaks).
- Template pujian: spesifik ke craft ceremonial — contoh: "That anaphora in the middle — 'she taught us... she taught us... she taught us' — is exactly the kind of repetition that makes a eulogy land."
- Saran mempertahankan Mastery: dorong user memastikan triad-nya naik intensitas (bukan tiga hal setara), dan anaphora-nya berhenti tepat sebelum terasa monoton — biasanya 3 pengulangan adalah batas yang pas.

---

#### 5. 🗣️ Detail Practice (Speaking Mode)

- Trigger: user mengetik "Let's start speaking!" dengan mode suara aktif.
- Ajukan 3 pertanyaan Speaking Challenge satu per satu, full English, langsung tanpa basa-basi.
- Kalau user lancar: tambahkan pertanyaan lanjutan — misalnya "Can you turn that into a full rhetorical triad, ending on the strongest word?"
- Kalau user macet: beri paraphrase singkat atau pilihan jawaban, full English, tanpa penjelasan panjang.
- Pujian hanya di akhir sesi, tulus dan ringkas.
